    <script type="text/javascript">
        function quoteImageLoadLater() {
            var elements = document.querySelectorAll('.bbcode-quote img');

            for(var count = 0; count < elements.length; count++) {
                var source_url = elements[count].src;

                console.log(document.readyState);
                console.log(source_url);

                if (source_url !== '') {
                    elements[count].setAttribute("data-src", source_url);
                    elements[count].removeAttribute('src');
                }
            }
        }

        var quoteImages = setInterval(function(){
            quoteImageLoadLater();
        }, 1);

        document.onreadystatechange = function () {
            if (document.readyState === 'interactive' || document.readyState == 'loading') {
                clearInterval(quoteImages);
                quoteImageLoadLater();
            }
        }

        window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            clearInterval(quoteImages);
            quoteImageLoadLater();
        }, false);
    </script>

<font face="Courier New"><font size="5"><font color="DeepSkyBlue">Features:</font></font><ul><li> Liquid Smooth</li>
<li> Pre-rooted with Magisk 16.0</li>
<li> Knox Container Removed</li>
<li> Basic Samsung Apps + Google App, Maps, YT &amp; Chrome</li>
<li> Flipboard &amp; Upday briefing</li>
<li> FM Radio</li>
<li> Samsung Music</li>
<li> Samsung Theme Support</li>
<li> Custom Kernel Support</li>
<li> April Security Patch</li>
<li> Camera Stickers</li>
<li> Oreo Emojis</li>
<li> <strike>Oreo Keyboard</strike></li>
<li> Black Boot anim+Splash for Silver, Gold and Rose Gold models</li>
<li> VoLTE in Nordic Countries</li>
</ul></font><br/>
<br/>
<font face="Courier New"><font size="5"><font color="DeepSkyBlue">Installation:</font></font></font><ul><li> Wipe Cache/dalvik, Data &amp; system</li>
<li> Flash latest Breeze+ build</li>
<li> Reboot</li>
<li> Device Automatically reboots, Yes It's Normal</li>
<li> Enjoy</li>
</ul><br/>

<div class="post-text" id="post_message_75139378">


<b>Important:</b><br/>
Do not report bugs if; you are using Substratum themes, Custom non store Samsung themes, xposed, SuperSU or any other rooting method than magisk. <br/>
<br/>
<b>Notes: </b><br/>
Live Message/Drawing won't be implemented 7.0 builds as live message.apk is targeted for 7.1.1 instead of 7.0 so the official apk's wont even install, and one's from XDA just make live display force close.


</div>

<div class="postbit-content postbit-content-moderated" id="td_post_75139938">








    <div class="postbit-posttitle smallfont">
        
        <strong>Any bugs found on this ROM</strong>
    </div>


<div class="post-text" id="post_message_75139938">


<div class="bbcode-quote">
	<div class="bbcode-quote-text">
		<div class="smallfont">Quote:</div>
		
			Originally Posted by <strong>Wizardlysense</strong>
			<a href="/galaxy-j5/samsung-galaxy-j5-pro-2017-roms-kernels-recoveries--other-development/breeze-os-j5y17lte-7-0-t3732878/post75139104" rel="nofollow" title="View Post"><i class="fas fa-caret-square-right"> </i></a>
		
		<p>* mod edit *</p>
	</div>
</div>
<div style="clear:left"></div>At the moment I'm using SimplifiedOS which made me face some little problems, like when typing the pin code to unlock the phone it keeps some seconds to unlock (this doesn't really bother me becouse I use fingerprint scanner) but anyways I'm looking for a stable, powerful, efficient and debloated ROM, so if anyone has tested this I'd like to know what is the experience with this ROM, thanks for your hard work guys! Keep it up, hope someone develop some AOSP ROM for this amazing device


</div>

<script>function b64EncodeUnicode(str){return btoa(encodeURIComponent(str).replace(/%([0-9A-F]{2})/g,function(match,p1){return String.fromCharCode('0x'+p1);}));}function b64DecodeUnicode(str){return decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(str)));}jQuery(document).ready(function($){var qrthread=$('#qr_threadid').val();var qrpost=$('#qr_postid').val();if($("input[name='loggedinuser']").val()==0)var isloggedin=false;else
var isloggedin=true;if($.cookie('qrcontent')){var existingqr=JSON.parse($.cookie('qrcontent'));if(existingqr.qrthread==qrthread){console.log("Matched QR thread cookie");$('#vB_Editor_QR_textarea').val(b64DecodeUnicode(existingqr.qrtext));$('html, body').animate({scrollTop:$('#vB_Editor_QR_textarea').offset().top-200},1000);$('#vB_Editor_QR_textarea').effect("highlight",{},3000).focus();}else{$.cookie('qrcontent',false,{expires:-1,path:'/'});}}$('#qr_submit').click(function(e){var qrtext=$('#vB_Editor_QR_textarea').val();var regex=new RegExp(/(http[s]?|www|(\[\/?(?:b|i|u|url|quote|code|img|color|size)*?.*?\]))/);if(qrtext==''){$.cookie('qrcontent','',{expires:-1,path:'/'});event.preventDefault();}else if(!isloggedin&&regex.test(qrtext)){event.preventDefault();$("#ajax_post_errors_message").html("Post contains a url or bbcode. Please remove and try submitting again.");$("#ajax_post_errors").show();$("#qr_posting_msg").hide();}else if(!isloggedin){var qrcontent={'qrtext':b64EncodeUnicode(qrtext),'qrpost':qrpost,'qrthread':qrthread};$.cookie('qrcontent',JSON.stringify(qrcontent),{expires:7,path:'/'});$.cookie('returnurl','https://forum.xda-developers.com/newreply.php?t='+qrthread,{expires:1,path:'/'});}});});</script>
